--
-- Table structure for table `apps_countries`
--

  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `country_code` varchar(2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `country_name` varchar(100) NOT NULL DEFAULT ''
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
